class="mw-body" id="content" role="main">\n   <a id="top">\n   </a>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="siteNotice">\n    <!-- CentralNotice -->\n   </div>\n   <div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n   </div>\n   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">\n    List of International Space Station visitors\n   </h1>\n   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n    <div class="noprint" id="siteSub">\n     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia\n    </div>\n    <div id="contentSub">\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">\n     Jump to:\n     <a href="#mw-head">\n      navigation\n     </a>\n     ,\n     <a href="#p-search">\n      search\n     </a>\n    </div>\n    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">\n     <div class="mw-parser-output">\n      <p>\n       This is a list of all visitors to the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       (ISS), including long-term crew, short-term visitors, and space tourists, in alphabetical order. ISS crew names are in\n       <b>\n        bold\n       </b>\n       . The suffix\n       <i>\n        (twice, thrice, ...)\n       </i>\n       refers to the individual\'s number of spaceflights to the ISS, not his or her total number of spaceflights. Entries without a flag symbol indicate that the individual was an American citizen at launch. Entries without a female symbol (\n       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Symbol_venus.svg">\n        <img alt="Symbol venus.svg" data-file-height="402" data-file-width="260" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Symbol_venus.svg/10px-Symbol_venus.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Symbol_venus.svg/15px-Symbol_venus.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Symbol_venus.svg/20px-Symbol_venus.svg.png 2x" width="10"/>\n       </a>\n       ) are men.\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Statistics">\n        Statistics\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Space_Station_visitors&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Statistics">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="floatright">\n       <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ISS_Visitors.png">\n        <img alt="ISS Visitors.png" data-file-height="477" data-file-width="940" height="203" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/3/38/ISS_Visitors.png/400px-ISS_Visitors.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/3/38/ISS_Visitors.png/600px-ISS_Visitors.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/3/38/ISS_Visitors.png/800px-ISS_Visitors.png 2x" width="400"/>\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As of July 28, 2017\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Space_Station_visitors&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , 227 individuals have made 393 spaceflights to the ISS, including the six people currently at the ISS (\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_52" title="Expedition 52">\n        Expedition 52\n       </a>\n       ). Two men made five spaceflights to the ISS, while five people made four, 29 people made three and 85 people made two. Note that this list assigns individuals with\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Dual_citizenship" title="Dual citizenship">\n        dual citizenship\n       </a>\n       to their country of primary residence at time of launch (for example, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">\n        Iranian\n       </a>\n       -\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n        American\n       </a>\n       space tourist\n       <a href="/wiki/Anousheh_Ansari" title="Anousheh Ansari">\n        Anousheh Ansari\n       </a>\n       is only listed under the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n        United States\n       </a>\n       ).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       All private space travel is aboard the Russian\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Soyuz_spacecraft" title="Soyuz spacecraft">\n        Soyuz spacecraft\n       </a>\n       . When only two crew members are required in the three seat Soyuz, and additional cargo is not sent, the additional seat is sold to the general public through\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Adventures" title="Space Adventures">\n        Space Adventures\n       </a>\n       . Private travelers remain on the ISS during handover from one expedition crew to the next, generally a week or two. The\n       <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n        NASA\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle" title="Space Shuttle">\n        Space Shuttle\n       </a>\n       carried seven crew members, and the longest docking with the ISS was 11 days. Many visitors to the ISS were accommodated for short periods during NASA shuttle dockings. NASA stated it was "not interested" in\n       <a href="/wiki/Private_spaceflight" title="Private spaceflight">\n        private spaceflight\n       </a>\n       from the beginning of the ISS and has not changed its position.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="Long-term_ISS_crew,_by_nationality">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Long-term_ISS_crew.2C_by_nationality">\n        Long-term ISS crew, by nationality\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_International_Space_Station_visitors&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Long-term ISS crew, by nationality">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">\n        <a srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/95/Tracy_Caldwell_Dyson_in_Cupola_ISS.jpg/450px-Tracy_Caldwell_Dyson_in_Cupola_ISS.jpg 1.5x, class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Tracy_Caldwell_Dyson_in_Cupola_ISS.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Tracy_Caldwell_Dyson" title="Tracy Caldwell Dyson">\n          Tracy Caldwell Dyson\n         </a>\n         in the\n         <a href="/wiki/Cupola_(ISS_module)" title="Cupola (ISS module)">\n          Cupola\n         </a>\n         module of the International Space Station observing\n         <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">\n          Earth\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Nationality\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         ISS Crew\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n
